MERGE (item:Item {name: "Wheat"})
SET item.level = 1,
    item.xp = 1,
    item.maxPrice = 3,
    item.productionTime = "2 min",
    item.imageUrl = "";

MERGE (location:ProductionLocation {name: "Field"})
MERGE (item:Item {name: "Wheat"})
MERGE (item)-[:PRODUCED_IN]->(location);

MATCH (item:Item {name: "Wheat"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Wheat"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 1}]->(ingredient);

MATCH (item:Item {name: "Fresh Porridge"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Pomegranate"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 1}]->(ingredient);

MATCH (item:Item {name: "Fresh Porridge"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Mint"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 2}]->(ingredient);

MATCH (item:Item {name: "Fresh Porridge"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Coconut"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 2}]->(ingredient);

MATCH (item:Item {name: "Fresh Porridge"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Oats"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 3}]->(ingredient);

MERGE (item:Item {name: "Vanilla Milkshake"})
SET item.level = 124,
    item.xp = 80,
    item.maxPrice = 673,
    item.productionTime = "45 min",
    item.imageUrl = "https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/hayday/images/1/14/Vanilla_Milkshake.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20240217094936";

MERGE (location:ProductionLocation {name: "Milkshake Bar"})
MERGE (item:Item {name: "Vanilla Milkshake"})
MERGE (item)-[:PRODUCED_IN]->(location);

MATCH (item:Item {name: "Vanilla Milkshake"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Vanilla Ice Cream"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 1}]->(ingredient);

MATCH (item:Item {name: "Vanilla Milkshake"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Cookie"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 2}]->(ingredient);

MATCH (item:Item {name: "Vanilla Milkshake"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Toffee"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 1}]->(ingredient);

MATCH (item:Item {name: "Vanilla Milkshake"})
MERGE (ingredient:Item {name: "Syrup"})
MERGE (item)-[:REQUIRES {amount: 1}]->(ingredient);

MERGE (item:Item {name: "Fruity Milkshake"})
SET item.level = 126,
    item.xp = 90,
    item.maxPrice = 759,
    item.productionTime = "35 min",
    item.imageUrl = "https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/hayday/images/f/fb/Fruity_Milkshake.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20240217095037";
